  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  1 34    (7)  Electronic mail addresses other than contact electronic
  1 35 mail addresses.
  2  1    (8)  Criminal or juvenile justice records.
  2  2    c.  Notwithstanding paragraph "b", information described in
  2  3 paragraph "b", subparagraphs (3), (5), (6), (7), and (8) may be
  2  4 kept in student data files by a school district or accredited
  2  5 nonpublic school, but shall not be shared with the department
  2  6 or any other governmental agency in this state.
  2  7    5.  a.  Student data shall be kept confidential by the
  2  8 department, a school district, or an accredited nonpublic
  2  9 school unless otherwise ordered by a court, by the lawful
  2 10 custodian of the data, or by another person duly authorized to
  2 11 release such data.
  2 12    b.  Except as provided in paragraph "a", student data shall
  2 13 not be provided outside of the state unless necessary to
  2 14 facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student who
  2 15 is transferring to a school outside the state.
  2 16    6.  Except as prohibited in subsection 7, the department
  2 17 shall establish and maintain a policy relating to the sharing,
  2 18 security, and confidentiality of student data in compliance
  2 19 with the federal Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act, 20
  2 20 U.S.C. {1232g.
  2 21    7.  The state board and the department shall not enter
  2 22 into an agreement with any entity that has an agreement with
  2 23 any federal governmental agency or with a third party that
  2 24 has an agreement with any federal governmental agency, to
  2 25 share personally identifiable student data, or that is working
  2 26 with any federal governmental agency to develop a strategy to
  2 27 make available, on an ongoing basis for research, personally
  2 28 identifiable student data that results from services provided
  2 29 by the entity to the state.
  2 30    8.  The department shall notify the governor and the general
  2 31 assembly annually of changes in measures to collect student
  2 32 data or to maintain student data collections by the department
  2 33 which are required for any reason, including changes in federal
  2 34 reporting requirements. The department shall not implement
  2 35 such change unless specifically authorized by a constitutional
  3  1 majority of each house of the general assembly and approved by
  3  2 the governor or unless otherwise specifically authorized by
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.

  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  2  4 kept in student data files by a school district or accredited
  2  5 nonpublic school, but shall not be shared with the department
  2  6 or any other governmental agency in this state.
  2  7    5.  a.  Student data shall be kept confidential by the
  2  8 department, a school district, or an accredited nonpublic
  2  9 school unless otherwise ordered by a court, by the lawful
  2 10 custodian of the data, or by another person duly authorized to
  2 11 release such data.
  2 12    b.  Except as provided in paragraph "a", student data shall
  2 13 not be provided outside of the state unless necessary to
  2 14 facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student who
  2 15 is transferring to a school outside the state.
  2 16    6.  Except as prohibited in subsection 7, the department
  2 17 shall establish and maintain a policy relating to the sharing,
  2 18 security, and confidentiality of student data in compliance
  2 19 with the federal Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act, 20
  2 20 U.S.C. {1232g.
  2 21    7.  The state board and the department shall not enter
  2 22 into an agreement with any entity that has an agreement with
  2 23 any federal governmental agency or with a third party that
  2 24 has an agreement with any federal governmental agency, to
  2 25 share personally identifiable student data, or that is working
  2 26 with any federal governmental agency to develop a strategy to
  2 27 make available, on an ongoing basis for research, personally
  2 28 identifiable student data that results from services provided
  2 29 by the entity to the state.
  2 30    8.  The department shall notify the governor and the general
  2 31 assembly annually of changes in measures to collect student
  2 32 data or to maintain student data collections by the department
  2 33 which are required for any reason, including changes in federal
  2 34 reporting requirements. The department shall not implement
  2 35 such change unless specifically authorized by a constitutional
  3  1 majority of each house of the general assembly and approved by
  3  2 the governor or unless otherwise specifically authorized by
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.

  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  2  9 school unless otherwise ordered by a court, by the lawful
  2 10 custodian of the data, or by another person duly authorized to
  2 11 release such data.
  2 12    b.  Except as provided in paragraph "a", student data shall
  2 13 not be provided outside of the state unless necessary to
  2 14 facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student who
  2 15 is transferring to a school outside the state.
  2 16    6.  Except as prohibited in subsection 7, the department
  2 17 shall establish and maintain a policy relating to the sharing,
  2 18 security, and confidentiality of student data in compliance
  2 19 with the federal Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act, 20
  2 20 U.S.C. {1232g.
  2 21    7.  The state board and the department shall not enter
  2 22 into an agreement with any entity that has an agreement with
  2 23 any federal governmental agency or with a third party that
  2 24 has an agreement with any federal governmental agency, to
  2 25 share personally identifiable student data, or that is working
  2 26 with any federal governmental agency to develop a strategy to
  2 27 make available, on an ongoing basis for research, personally
  2 28 identifiable student data that results from services provided
  2 29 by the entity to the state.
  2 30    8.  The department shall notify the governor and the general
  2 31 assembly annually of changes in measures to collect student
  2 32 data or to maintain student data collections by the department
  2 33 which are required for any reason, including changes in federal
  2 34 reporting requirements. The department shall not implement
  2 35 such change unless specifically authorized by a constitutional
  3  1 majority of each house of the general assembly and approved by
  3  2 the governor or unless otherwise specifically authorized by
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.

  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  2 14 facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student who
  2 15 is transferring to a school outside the state.
  2 16    6.  Except as prohibited in subsection 7, the department
  2 17 shall establish and maintain a policy relating to the sharing,
  2 18 security, and confidentiality of student data in compliance
  2 19 with the federal Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act, 20
  2 20 U.S.C. {1232g.
  2 21    7.  The state board and the department shall not enter
  2 22 into an agreement with any entity that has an agreement with
  2 23 any federal governmental agency or with a third party that
  2 24 has an agreement with any federal governmental agency, to
  2 25 share personally identifiable student data, or that is working
  2 26 with any federal governmental agency to develop a strategy to
  2 27 make available, on an ongoing basis for research, personally
  2 28 identifiable student data that results from services provided
  2 29 by the entity to the state.
  2 30    8.  The department shall notify the governor and the general
  2 31 assembly annually of changes in measures to collect student
  2 32 data or to maintain student data collections by the department
  2 33 which are required for any reason, including changes in federal
  2 34 reporting requirements. The department shall not implement
  2 35 such change unless specifically authorized by a constitutional
  3  1 majority of each house of the general assembly and approved by
  3  2 the governor or unless otherwise specifically authorized by
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.

  2 23 any federal governmental agency or with a third party that
  2 24 has an agreement with any federal governmental agency, to
  2 25 share personally identifiable student data, or that is working
  2 26 with any federal governmental agency to develop a strategy to
  2 27 make available, on an ongoing basis for research, personally
  2 28 identifiable student data that results from services provided
  2 29 by the entity to the state.
  2 30    8.  The department shall notify the governor and the general
  2 31 assembly annually of changes in measures to collect student
  2 32 data or to maintain student data collections by the department
  2 33 which are required for any reason, including changes in federal
  2 34 reporting requirements. The department shall not implement
  2 35 such change unless specifically authorized by a constitutional
  3  1 majority of each house of the general assembly and approved by
  3  2 the governor or unless otherwise specifically authorized by
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj

  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  2 25 share personally identifiable student data, or that is working
  2 26 with any federal governmental agency to develop a strategy to
  2 27 make available, on an ongoing basis for research, personally
  2 28 identifiable student data that results from services provided
  2 29 by the entity to the state.
  2 30    8.  The department shall notify the governor and the general
  2 31 assembly annually of changes in measures to collect student
  2 32 data or to maintain student data collections by the department
  2 33 which are required for any reason, including changes in federal
  2 34 reporting requirements. The department shall not implement
  2 35 such change unless specifically authorized by a constitutional
  3  1 majority of each house of the general assembly and approved by
  3  2 the governor or unless otherwise specifically authorized by
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj

  2 28 identifiable student data that results from services provided
  2 29 by the entity to the state.

  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  2 32 data or to maintain student data collections by the department
  2 33 which are required for any reason, including changes in federal
  2 34 reporting requirements. The department shall not implement
  2 35 such change unless specifically authorized by a constitutional
  3  1 majority of each house of the general assembly and approved by
  3  2 the governor or unless otherwise specifically authorized by
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.

  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  3  3 statute.
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.
  3  7    10.  This section shall not be construed to do any of the
  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,
  3 10 subsection 44, or chapter 256H.
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  3  4    9.  Except as provided in subsection 5, the department shall
  3  5 not publish or share with any governmental agency outside of
  3  6 the state student data except in aggregate form.

  3  8 following:
  3  9    a.  Supersede any provision of section 22.7, section 256.9,

  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent

  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's

  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  3 11    b.  Undermine or eliminate the right of a student's parent
  3 12 or guardian to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the
  3 13 student's information on the department's database, or the
  3 14 student's future right as an adult to review, correct, amend,
  3 15 add to, or delete the student's information on the department's
  3 16 database.
  3 17                           EXPLANATION
  3 18 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.

  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools

  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  3 19 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  3 20    This bill relates to student data collection by the
  3 21 department of education, school districts, and accredited
  3 22 nonpublic schools. The bill requires the department to create
  3 23 student data=related policies and plans, and prohibits the
  3 24 department from making changes in the measures used to collect
  3 25 or maintain student data unless specifically authorized by the
  3 26 general assembly and approved by the governor or by statute.
  3 27    The bill requires the department to annually conduct an
  3 28 inventory of and categorize the data collected on students
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.

  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
       LSB 5705YH (3) 87
       kh/rj
  3 29 and the purposes for which the data is collected, and report
  3 30 its findings and recommendations to the general assembly by
  3 31 November 1, 2018, and by November 1 each succeeding year.
  3 32    The bill prohibits, except as otherwise provided, the
  3 33 department, school districts, and accredited nonpublic schools
  3 34 from including in student data files certain information
  3 35 regarding biometric and psychometric data; certain information
  4  1 concerning the student's or the student's family; and further
  4  2 prohibits the department from publishing or sharing with any
  4  3 governmental agency outside of the state student data except
  4  4 in aggregate form.
  4  5    Student data must be kept confidential unless otherwise
  4  6 ordered by a court, by the lawful custodian of the records, or
  4  7 by another person duly authorized to release such information.
  4  8 Student data may be provided outside of the state if necessary
  4  9 to facilitate the timely enrollment and placement of a student
  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.

  4 10 who is transferring to an out=of=state school.
  4 11    The department must establish and maintain a policy relating
  4 12 to the sharing, security, and confidentiality of student data
  4 13 in compliance with the federal Family Educational Rights
  4 14 and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. {1232g.  The state board and the
  4 15 department are prohibited from entering into an agreement with
  4 16 any entity that has an agreement with any federal governmental
  4 17 agency or with a third party that has an agreement with any
  4 18 federal governmental agency, to share personally identifiable
  4 19 student data, or that is working with any federal governmental
  4 20 agency to develop a strategy to make available, on an ongoing
  4 21 basis for research, personally identifiable student data that
  4 22 results from services provided by the entity to the state.
  4 23    The department shall notify the governor and the general
  4 24 assembly annually of changes to existing student data
  4 25 collections maintained by the department. Unless specifically
  4 26 authorized by the general assembly and approved by the governor
  4 27 or by statute, changes that are not necessitated by changes
  4 28 in state and federal reporting requirements shall not be
  4 29 implemented.
  4 30    The new provisions relating to student data shall not be
  4 31 construed to undermine or eliminate the right of a student's
  4 32 parent or guardian, or the student's future right as an adult,
  4 33 to review, correct, amend, add to, or delete the student's
  4 34 information on the department's database; or construed to
  4 35 supersede any existing open records law provisions, provisions
  5  1 relating to the department's comprehensive management
  5  2 information system which are in compliance with state and
  5  3 federal reporting requirements, or provisions enacting the
  5  4 interstate compact on educational opportunity for military
  5  5 children.
